2025-10-01T17:49:30Z — MCP creds: service and usage (manager summary)
- Service: Internal MCP backend API at MCP_API_URL; not Shopify/GA4 directly.
- Auth: Authorization: Bearer MCP_API_KEY. Live mode requires ENABLE_MCP=1 and USE_MOCK_DATA=0.
- Endpoints: GET /health; POST /recommendations; POST /inventory/signals; POST /seo/opportunities.
- Headers: X-Shop-Domain, X-MCP-Resource, X-Request-Id, X-MCP-Client-Version, X-MCP-Features.
- Payload: { resource, shopDomain, params?, dateRange? } -> McpResponse<T>.
- Validation plan: run dashboard/app/lib/mcp/__tests__/live-connection.test.ts (auto-skips if env absent). One-shot ephemeral command provided in feedback/mcp.md.
- Status: Awaiting MCP_API_URL and MCP_API_KEY to execute live test. Mock-mode suites are green; syntax error fixed in app/lib/mcp/index.ts; protocol-contract tests passing.
